(3*x^2 + 8*x - 9)/(x^3 + 4*x^2 - 9*x - 36) = 1/(x + 4) + 1/(x + 3) + 1/(x - 3)
(2*x^2 + 10*x + 1)/(x^3 + 5*x^2 - 8*x - 48) = 1/(x + 4) + 1/(x - 3) + 1/(x + 4)^2
(2*x^2 + 5*x + 8)/(x^3 + 4*x^2 + 4*x + 16) = (x + 1)/(x^2 + 4) + 1/(x + 4)
(10*x^2 + 7*x + 9)/(x^3 + x^2 - x + 2) = (5*x + 2)/(x^2 - x + 1) + 5/(x + 2)
(-2*x^2 + 7*x - 10)/(x^3 - 4*x^2 + 4*x - 3) = -(x - 3)/(x^2 - x + 1) - 1/(x - 3)
(-6*x^2 + 3*x)/(x^3 - x^2 + x - 6) = -(4*x + 3)/(x^2 + x + 3) - 2/(x - 2)
(4*x^2 - 5*x + 7)/(x^3 - 2*x^2 + 3*x - 2) = (x - 1)/(x^2 - x + 2) + 3/(x - 1)
(5*x^2 + 7*x + 7)/(x^3 + 2*x + 3) = 4*(x + 1)/(x^2 - x + 3) + 1/(x + 1)
(-2*x^2 - 2*x - 5)/(x^3 - x^2 + 2*x - 2) = (x - 1)/(x^2 + 2) - 3/(x - 1)
(5*x^2 + 2*x - 4)/(x^3 - x^2 - 4*x + 4) = 1/(x + 2) - 1/(x - 1) + 5/(x - 2)
(4*x^2 - 2*x - 6)/(x^3 - 3*x^2 + 7*x - 5) = (5*x + 1)/(x^2 - 2*x + 5) - 1/(x - 1)
(-2*x^2 - 9*x + 6)/(x^3 + 8*x^2 + 21*x + 20) = -(4*x + 1)/(x^2 + 4*x + 5) + 2/(x + 4)
(-7*x^2 + 4*x + 3)/(x^3 - x^2 - 9*x - 12) = -(4*x + 3)/(x^2 + 3*x + 3) - 3/(x - 4)
(2*x^2 + 5*x - 10)/(x^3 + 2*x^2 + 2*x + 4) = (4*x - 3)/(x^2 + 2) - 2/(x + 2)
(8*x^2 - 3*x + 10)/(x^3 + 8) = (4*x - 3)/(x^2 - 2*x + 4) + 4/(x + 2)
(-3*x^2 + 3*x - 2)/(x^3 - 4*x^2 + 7*x - 4) = -2*(x + 1)/(x^2 - 3*x + 4) - 1/(x - 1)
(-x^2 + 7*x - 5)/(x^3 - 7*x^2 + 15*x - 12) = -2*(x - 1)/(x^2 - 3*x + 3) + 1/(x - 4)
